//To get away from the menu screen
RegisterEvent Engine RETURN 2
RegisterEvent Engine failed 3
RegisterEvent Engine passed 4

//the main character


InsertMesh Car Car.X
SetPosition Car 551.8		0.0		918.2
SetOrientation Car 0.0 1.57 0.0
SetMass Car 1.0
SetMassMoment Car 100.0 200.0 100.0
RegisterEvent Car tick 1
RegisterEvent Car LEFT 1
RegisterEvent Car RIGHT 1
RegisterEvent Car SPACE 1
RegisterEvent Car B 1
RegisterEvent Car collision 2
AddBoundary Car 10.0 -10.0  20.0 0.0  26.0 -12.0  0

//Sounds
InsertSound  soundCountdown sound/Countdown.wav
RegisterEvent soundCountdown H 1

InsertSound  soundHorn sound/horn.wav
RegisterEvent soundHorn UP 1

InsertSound  soundCollision sound/mepaintwork.wav
RegisterEvent soundCollision scrape 1

InsertSound  soundDamage sound/crash.wav
RegisterEvent soundDamage damage 1

InsertSound soundPassed sound/gooddel3.wav
RegisterEvent soundPassed passed 1

InsertSound soundBrake sound/brake.wav
RegisterEvent soundBrake B 1

InsertSound soundAccel sound/accel.wav
RegisterEvent soundAccel SPACE 1






//Camera and rules
